This notebook shows how to use an agent to compare two documents. The high level idea is we will create a question-answering chain for each document, and then use that  This type of agent allows calling multiple functions at once. This is really useful when some steps can be computed in parallel - like when asked to compare multiple documents IntegrationsCallbacksChat modelsChat loadersDocument loadersDocument
